Buy 1\n        tx = self.client.post(\n            \"/transactions\",\n            json={\"product_id\": prod_id, \"amount\": 1},\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {user_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(tx.status_code, 200)\n        tx_data = tx.json()\n        self.assertEqual(tx_data[\"product_id\"], prod_id)\n        self.assertEqual(tx_data[\"amount\"], 1)\n        self.assertAlmostEqual(tx_data[\"total_price\"], 25.0)\n\n        # Stock decreased\n        get_prod = self.client.get(f\"/products/{prod_id}\")\n        self.assertEqual(get_prod.json()[\"stock\"], 1)\n\n        # User can see their transaction\n        txs = self.client.get(\n            \"/transactions/me\",\n            headers={\"Authorization\": f\"Bearer {user_token}\"}\n        )\n        self.assertEqual(txs.status_code, 200)\n        self.assertEqual(len(txs.json()), 1)\n\n        # Login with wrong password\n        r4 = login_user(\"alice\", \"wrongpass\")\n        self.assertEqual(r4.status_code, 400)\n        self.assertIn(\"Incorrect username or password\", r4.json()[\"detail\"])\n\n        # Login with non-existent user\n        r5 = login_user(\"bob\", \"password123\")\n        self.assertEqual(r5.status_code, 400)\n        self.assertIn(\"Incorrect username or password\", r5.json()[\"detail\"])\n\n    def test_password_length_constraints(self):\n        # Manually set role to admin in DB\n            user = self.db.query(User).filter(User.username == username).first()\n            user.role = \"admin\"\n            self.db.commit()\n        return response\n\n    def login_user(self, username, password):\n        response = self.client.post(\n            \"/token\",\n            data={\"username\": username, \"password\": password},\n            headers={\"Content-Type\": \"application/x-www-form-urlencoded\"},\n        )\n        return response\n\n    def create_product(self, token, name=\"TestProduct\", price=10.0, description=\"\", stock=10):\n        response = self.client.post(\n            \"/products\",\n            json={\"name\": name, \"price\": price, \"description\": description, \"stock\": stock},\n            headers=get_auth_headers(token),\n        )\n        return response\n\n    def make_transaction(self, token, product_id, amount):\n        response = self.client.post(\n            \"/transactions\",\n            json={\"product_id\": product_id, \"amount\": amount},\n            headers=get_auth_headers(token),\n        )\n        return response\n\n    # HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=\"Amount must be positive\")\n    if product.stock < tx.amount:\n        raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail=\"Insufficient stock\")\n    total_price =
